Deep Search understands code semantically — it traces call chains, data flows, and architectural relationships across files. It is **far more effective** than keyword search for understanding how code fits together.

**When to use Deep Search (mandatory for all of these):**
- Understanding how a feature or subsystem works end-to-end
- Tracing data flow or request lifecycle across multiple files
- Finding all the places that need to change for a cross-cutting modification
- Understanding architectural relationships before making changes
- Any time you need to understand "how does X work?" or "what calls Y?"

**Use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_deepsearch_read`** to retrieve the full content of any Deep Search result.

Do NOT skip Deep Search and jump straight to keyword search or file browsing. Deep Search gives you the architectural context you need to solve the task correctly.

    11→NCCLComm::NCCLComm(ncclComm_t ncclComm) : ncclComm_(ncclComm) {}
    12→
    13→NCCLComm::~NCCLComm() noexcept {
    14→  // (kwen2501) Making CUDA/NCCL calls in this destructor can hit CUDA driver
    15→  // shutdown error if CUDA context has exited first. Thus, we are not
    16→  // destroying or aborting NCCL communicators here. We just detect and warn
    17→  // about the risk of memory leak. Normally, a user would have called
    18→  // `destroy_process_group` or `abort_process_group`, and such risk would be
    19→  // avoided.
    20→  LockType lock(mutex_);
    21→  if (ncclComm_ && initialized_ && !aborted_) {
    22→    TORCH_WARN_ONCE(
    23→        "WARNING: NCCL communicator hasn't been destroyed. This may cause "
    24→        "memory leaks. To avoid the risk, you can call `destroy_process_group` "
    25→        "during normal exit or `_abort_process_group` when handling failures.")
    26→  }
    27→}
    28→
    29→// NOLINTNEXTLINE(*-noexcept-move-*)
    30→NCCLComm::NCCLComm(NCCLComm&& other) {
    31→  // Using other's lock, as it reads other's states
    32→  // Can not use this.mutex_, as this object is being constructed.
    33→  LockType lock(other.mutex_);
    34→  std::swap(ncclComm_, other.ncclComm_);
    35→  std::swap(aborted_, other.aborted_);
    36→  std::swap(ncclAsyncErr_, other.ncclAsyncErr_);
    37→  std::swap(initialized_, other.initialized_);
    38→  std::swap(nonBlocking_, other.nonBlocking_);
    39→  std::swap(deviceIndex_, other.deviceIndex_);
    40→}

1. **In NCCLUtils.hpp**:

   - The `abort()` method was rewritten similarly (lines 370-439)

104-assistanttext-
I have successfully implemented the fix for the thread safety issue when calling `ncclCommGetAsyncError`. Here's a summary of what was done:

## Summary of Changes

### Issue
The NCCL library does not provide thread-safety guarantees for `ncclCommGetAsyncError`. When both the main thread and watchdog thread call this function concurrently on the same communicator, it can lead to race conditions and undefined behavior.

### Solution
Added thread safety by:

1. **New `NCCLComm::getAsyncError()` method** (`NCCLUtils.hpp:363-368`, `NCCLUtils.cpp:470-473`)
   - Added a thread-safe wrapper that acquires the mutex before calling `ncclCommGetAsyncError`

2. **Updated `C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE` macro** (`NCCLUtils.hpp:135-156`)
   - Changed parameter from raw `comm` to `commWrapper` (NCCLComm pointer)
   - Now calls `commWrapper->getAsyncError(&result)` instead of `ncclCommGetAsyncError(comm, &result)`
   - Added documentation comment explaining thread safety

3. **Updated `C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_GROUPEND` macro** (`NCCLUtils.hpp:178-196`)
   - Changed from `ncclCommGetAsyncError(comm->getNcclComm(), &state)` to `comm->getAsyncError(&state)`

4. **Rewrote `NCCLComm::waitReady()`** (`NCCLUtils.cpp:180-214`)
   - Inlined the wait loop instead of using the macro
   - Since this method already holds the mutex, it safely calls `ncclCommGetAsyncError` directly
   - Added comment explaining the thread safety

5. **Rewrote `NCCLComm::abort()`** (`NCCLUtils.cpp:400-426`)
   - Similar to waitReady(), inlined the wait loop
   - Already holds the mutex, so calls `ncclCommGetAsyncError` directly
   - Added comment explaining the thread safety

6. **Fixed `NCCLComm::split()`** (`NCCLUtils.cpp:253-256`)
   - Changed from passing `sourceComm` (raw `ncclComm_t`) to `source` (NCCLComm pointe
... (truncated)

mapping).\n        return ncclMax;\n      }\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_AVG\n      if (reduceOp == ReduceOp::AVG) {\n        C10_THROW_ERROR(\n            TypeError, \"Cannot use ReduceOp.AVG with boolean inputs\");\n      }\n#endif // NCCL_HAS_AVG\n    }\n    if (reduceOp == ReduceOp::PREMUL_SUM) {\n#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_PREMUL_SUM_SUPPORT\n      switch (dataType) {\n        case ncclHalf:\n          return unpackPreMulSum<at::Half, ncclHalf>(reduceOp, comm);\n        case ncclFloat:\n          return unpackPreMulSum<float, ncclFloat>(reduceOp, comm);\n        case ncclBfloat16:\n          return unpackPreMulSum<float, ncclBfloat16>(reduceOp, comm);\n        case ncclDouble:\n          return unpackPreMulSum<double, ncclDouble>(reduceOp, comm);\n        default:\n          C10_THROW_ERROR(\n              TypeError,\n              \"PreMulSum Data type must be half, float, bfloat16 or double\");\n          return ncclRedOp_t{};\n      }\n#else\n      C10_THROW_ERROR(ValueError, \"PreMulSum requires NCCL>=2.11.1\");\n#endif // ENABLE_NCCL_PREMUL_SUM_SUPPORT\n    }\n    return ncclOp.at(reduceOp);\n  } catch (const std::out_of_range&) {\n    switch (reduceOp) {\n      case ReduceOp::AVG:\n        C10_THROW_ERROR(\n            ValueError,\n            c10::str(\n                \"AVG requires NCCL 2.10+. The current version is \",\n                NCCL_MAJOR,\n                \".\",\n                NCCL_MINOR));\n        break;\n      case ReduceOp::BAND:\n        C10_THROW_ERROR(ValueError, \"Cannot use ReduceOp.BAND with NCCL\");\n        break;\n      case ReduceOp::BOR:\n        C10_THROW_ERROR(ValueError, \"Cannot use ReduceOp.BOR with NCCL\");\n        break;\n      case ReduceOp::BXOR:\n        C10_THROW_ERROR(ValueError, \"Cannot use ReduceOp.BXOR with NCCL\");\n        break;\n      default:\n        C10_THROW_ERROR(ValueError, \"Unhandled ReduceOp\");\n        break;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// Get a key string from device\ninline std::string getKeyFromDevice(const at::Device& device) {\n  return std::to_string(device.index());\n}\n\nstd::string getKeySendRecv(int myRank, int peer) {\n  int lowRank = myRank < peer ? myRank : peer;\n  int highRank = myRank < peer ? peer : myRank;\n  std::string sendRecvPair =\n      std::to_string(lowRank) + \":\" + std::to_string(highRank);\n  return sendRecvPair;\n}\n\n// Get device from tensor\ninline at::Device getDevice(at::Tensor& tensor) {\n  return tensor.device();\n}\n\n// [Sync Streams] Helper that lets the input ncclStreams to wait for the current\n// stream. NCCL communications run on ncclStreams, but input tensors are\n// allocated on different streams (i.e., current streams). Communications on\n// ncclStreams cannot start before pending input tensor ops on current streams\n// finish. Otherwise, ops on two streams might read/write same tensors\n// concurrently.\n//\n// The synchronization above alone is not enough. We also need to make sure\n// input tensors are not freed before their usages on ncclStreams finish. This\n// can be achieved by calling c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::recordStream,\n// which remembers the usage stream (ncclStream), creates an event on the usage\n// stream when GC attempts to free the input tensor, and delays GC until that\n// event is done.\nvoid syncStream(\n    at::Device& device,\n    at::cuda::CUDAEvent& ncclEvent,\n    at::cuda::CUDAStream& ncclStream) {\n  ncclEvent.record(at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream(device.index()));\n  ncclEvent.block(ncclStream);\n}\n\nstd::string getNcclAbortedCommStoreKey(const std::string& ncclIdStr) {\n  return std::string(kNCCLAbortedCommStoreKey) + \":\" + ncclIdStr;\n}\n\n// Returns exception's what() given an exception_ptr instance.\nstd::string getExceptionMsgFromExceptionPtr(\n    const std::exception_ptr& exceptionPtr) {\n  TORCH_CHECK(exceptionPtr != nullptr);\n  try {\n    std::rethrow_exception(exceptionPtr);\n  } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n    return e.what();\n  } catch (...) {\n    return \"Unknown exception type\";\n  }\n}\n\ninline void errorIfCapturingNonCapturableNCCL(c10::cuda::CaptureStatus status) {\n  // parentheses avoid some compiler warnings\n  static const uint64_t min_version =\n      (((uint64_t)2) << 32) + (((uint64_t)9) << 16) + ((uint64_t)6);\n  static const uint64_t cur_version = torch::cuda::nccl::version();\n  if (cur_version < min_version) {\n    TORCH_CHECK_WITH(\n        NotImplementedError,\n        status == c10::cuda::CaptureStatus::None,\n        \"Capturing NCCL collectives is only allowed with NCCL >= 2.9.6\");\n  }\n}\n\n// When TORCH_NCCL_USE_TENSOR_REGISTER_ALLOCATOR_HOOK is set, all tensors (no\n// matter how they have been allocated) are registered with all NCCL comms.\nbool shouldAllCommunicatorsRegisterAllTensors() {\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER\n  static const bool flag = [] {\n    const bool flag =\n        getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_USE_TENSOR_REGISTER_ALLOCATOR_HOOK, false);\n    if (flag &&\n        c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::CUDAAllocatorConfig::\n            expandable_segments()) {\n      LOG(INFO)\n          << \"disables TORCH_NCCL_USE_TENSOR_REGISTER_ALLOCATOR_HOOK because it is not compatible with CUDA allocator expandable segments mode.\";\n      return false;\n    }\n    return flag;\n  }();\n  return flag;\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif // NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER\n}\n\n} // namespace\n\n// Map each communicator to the memory pools registered with it.\n// This map is used when the caching allocator allocates or frees segments, in\n// order to register or deregister them with the relevant NCCL communicators.\n// There are two modes to do so:\n// - If TORCH_NCCL_USE_TENSOR_REGISTER_ALLOCATOR_HOOK=1 then *ALL* segments\n//   will be registered with *ALL* NCCL communicators (for the same device),\n//   even if they were allocated with cudaMalloc (which NCCL doesn't like).\n// - If a MemPool is explicitly registered with a ProcessGroup, then all its\n//   segments (current and future) will be registered with the NCCL communicator\n//   corresponding to the pool's device. This works best if the MemPool is set\n//   up to use ncclMemAlloc (which is exposed by the ProcessGroup).\n// Implementation notes:\n// - We cannot reuse devNCCLCommMap_ in each ProcessGroup because the key may be\n//   ranks rather than device in point-to-point case.\n// - This map has also to be maintained as global variable since the register\n//   hooks are called outside the scope of any PG, thus we need traverse\n//   communicators in all PGs.\n\n// MemPoolSet has ids of mempools used with this communicator, and whether they\n// were registered with window APIs or not\nusing MemPoolSet = std::unordered_set<\n    std::tuple<c10::cuda::MempoolId_t, bool>,\n    c10::hash<std::tuple<c10::cuda::MempoolId_t, bool>>>;\nstatic std::unordered_map<std::shared_ptr<NCCLComm>, MemPoolSet>\n    ncclCommMemPoolMap;\nstatic std::mutex ncclCommMemPoolMapMutex;\n\nstd::atomic<bool> ProcessGroupNCCL::shouldDump_(false);\n\nstatic void cacheAllocatorRegisterHook(\n    const c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::TraceEntry& te) {\n  // Register after SEGMENT_ALLOC\n  if (te.action_ !=\n      c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::TraceEntry::Action::SEGMENT_ALLOC) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(ncclCommMemPoolMapMutex);\n  for (auto& [ncclComm, memPools] : ncclCommMemPoolMap) {\n    if (te.device_ == ncclComm->getDeviceIndex()) {\n      bool symm = false;\n      bool should_register = shouldAllCommunicatorsRegisterAllTensors();\n      auto it =\n          std::find_if(memPools.begin(), memPools.end(), [&](const auto& tup) {\n            return std::get<0>(tup) == te.mempool_;\n          });\n      if (it != memPools.end()) {\n        should_register = true;\n        symm = std::get<1>(*it);\n      }\n      if (should_register) {\n        // NOLINTNEXTLINE(performance-no-int-to-ptr)\n        ncclComm->registerSegment(\n            reinterpret_cast<void*>(te.addr_),\n            te.size_,\n            /*errorOnRereg*/ false,\n            /*window*/ symm);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nstatic void cacheAllocatorDeregisterHook(\n    const c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::TraceEntry& te) {\n  // deregister before SEGMENT_FREE\n  if (te.action_ !=\n      c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::TraceEntry::Action::SEGMENT_FREE) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(ncclCommMemPoolMapMutex);\n  for (auto& [ncclComm, memPools] : ncclCommMemPoolMap) {\n    if (te.device_ == ncclComm->getDeviceIndex()) {\n      bool symm = false;\n      bool should_register = shouldAllCommunicatorsRegisterAllTensors();\n      auto it =\n          std::find_if(memPools.begin(), memPools.end(), [&](const auto& tup) {\n            return std::get<0>(tup) == te.mempool_;\n          });\n      if (it != memPools.end()) {\n        should_register = true;\n        symm = std::get<1>(*it);\n      }\n      if (should_register) {\n        // NOLINTNEXTLINE(performance-no-int-to-ptr)\n        ncclComm->deregisterSegment(reinterpret_cast<void*>(te.addr_), symm);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nstatic void attachAllocatorHooks() {\n  static auto flag [[maybe_unused]] = [] {\n    // Attaching hooks fails if CUDACachingAllocator is not initialized, so\n    // Init for CUDA is called (and is a no-op if CUDA is already\n    // initialized).\n    at::globalContext().lazyInitDevice(c10::DeviceType::CUDA);\n    c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::attachAllocatorTraceTracker(\n        &cacheAllocatorRegisterHook);\n    c10::cuda::CUDACachingAllocator::attachAllocatorTraceTracker(\n        &cacheAllocatorDeregisterHook);\n    return true;\n  }();\n}\n\nstatic std::\n    unordered_map<std::string, std::unordered_map<std::string, std::string>>\n    getNCCLCommDumpMap() {\n#if (defined(IS_NCCLX) || defined(USE_ROCM)) && defined(NCCL_COMM_DUMP)\n  std::unordered_map<\n      std::string /* ncclUniqueID */,\n      std::unordered_map<std::string, std::string> /* dump from this comm */>\n      ncclDumpMap;\n  // dump_nccl_trace is only called from the default PG (local_id_=0), but we\n  // reset_nccl_trace() {\n  FlightRecorderCUDA::get()->reset_all();\n}\n\nstd::string dump_nccl_trace(\n    bool includeCollectives,\n    bool includeStackTraces,\n    bool onlyActive) {\n  auto C10_THROW_ERROR(NotImplementedError, \"WorkNCCL::isSuccess() is deprecated\");\n}\n\nvoid ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::checkAndSetException() {\n  if (exception()) {\n    // We already have an exception.\n    return;\n  }\n\n  auto exception_ptr = checkForNCCLErrors();\n  std::unique_lock<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n  exception_ = exception_ptr;\n  if (exception_) {\n    LOG(ERROR) << logPrefix() << \"Collective \" << *this\n               << \" raised the following async exception: \"\n               << getExceptionMsgFromExceptionPtr(exception_);\n\n    // Mark future result as ERROR\n    if (futureWorkResult_ && !futureWorkResult_->completed()) {\n      futureWorkResult_->markCompleted(\n          at::IValue(static_cast<uint8_t>(WorkResult::COMM_ERROR)));\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nconst std::string& ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::logPrefix() const {\n  static std::string prefix = c10::str(\"[Rank \", rank_, \"] \");\n  return prefix;\n}\n\nvoid if the NCCL kernels are completed on the GPUs\nbool ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::finishedGPUExecution() {\n  checkAndSetException();\n  return finishedGPUExecutionInternal();\n}\n\nbool ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::startedGPUExecutionInternal() const {\n  // if timing is disabled we won't have allocated start events\n  if (!timingEnabled_) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  // Checking the work's corresponding CUDA event's status\n  if (!ncclStartEvent_->query()) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::finishedGPUExecutionInternal() const {\n  // Checking the work's corresponding CUDA event's status\n  // It calls `cudaEventQuery` eventually. Although this seems to be a\n  // non-blocking call, but we did notice hangs in the past. It can\n  // hang if another thread is holding the CUDA global context lock. For\n  // example, when doing a `cudaDeviceSynchronize` or even\n  // `cudaStreamSynchronize`.\n  if (!ncclEndEvent_->query()) {\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::checkTimeout(\n    std::optional<std::chrono::milliseconds> timeout) {\n  STATIC_SCOPED_WAIT_COUNTER(\n      pytorch.wait_counter.ProcessGroupNCCL__checkTimeout);\n  auto currentTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n  auto timeElapsed = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(\n      currentTimepoint - workStartTime_);\n  auto workTimeout = timeout ? *timeout : opTimeout_;\n\n  if (timeElapsed < workTimeout) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  // Timed out\n\n  std::string exceptionMsg = c10::str(\n      logPrefix(),\n      \"Watchdog caught collective operation timeout: \",\n      *this,\n      \" ran for \",\n      timeElapsed.count(),\n      \" milliseconds before timing out.\");\n\n  LOG(ERROR) << exceptionMsg;\n\n  std::exception_ptr exception_ptr =\n      std::make_exception_ptr(C10_BUILD_ERROR(DistBackendError, exceptionMsg));\n  if (!exception()) {\n    // if there is already an error, we don't override it\n    setException(exception_ptr);\n  }\n\n  // Mark future result as TIMEOUT\n  if (futureWorkResult_ && !futureWorkResult_->completed()) {\n    futureWorkResult_->markCompleted(\n        at::IValue(static_cast<uint8_t>(WorkResult::TIMEOUT)));\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\n// Print the traceback of the collective at call time\nstd::string ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::getTraceback() const {\n  // First step we get the corresponding record entry from FR, based on work's\n  // trace_id_ and trace_reset_epoch_\n  std::optional<FlightRecorderCUDA::Entry> entry =\n      FlightRecorderCUDA::get()->getEntry(trace_id_, trace_reset_epoch_);\n  if (entry.has_value()) {\n    auto entryVal = entry.value();\n    // Get stack trace from FR entry, in string format\n    // Note: `getTraceback` call below invokes `torch::symbolize`, which may\n    // need to acquire the GIL. In order for watchdog to be block-free, we make\n    // the call with std::async.\n    auto future = std::async(\n        std::launch::async, [&entryVal]() { return entryVal.getTraceback(); });\n    // Wait for the future to complete or timeout\n    auto status = future.wait_for(std::chrono::seconds(8));\n    if (status == std::future_status::ready) {\n      return future.get();\n    }\n  }\n  return \"\";\n}\n\n// Print the traceback of the collective at call time\nvoid ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::printTraceback() const {\n  std::string tracebackStr = getTraceback();\n  if (!tracebackStr.empty()) {\n    LOG(ERROR) << \"Stack trace of the failed collective: \\n\" << tracebackStr;\n  } // else, symbolizer probably timed out, we skip logging the stack trace.\n  else {\n    LOG(ERROR)\n        << \"Stack trace of the failed collective not found, \"\n        << \"potentially because FlightRecorder is disabled. \"\n        << \"You can enable it by setting TORCH_NCCL_TRACE_BUFFER_SIZE to a non-zero value.\";\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::handleException(\n    ErrorHandlingMode errorHandling) {\n  if (exception_) {\n    auto exceptionMsg = c10::str(\n        \"Some NCCL operations have failed or timed out. Due to the \",\n        \"asynchronous nature of CUDA kernels, subsequent GPU operations \",\n        \"might run on corrupted/incomplete data.\");\n    LOG(ERROR) << logPrefix() << exceptionMsg;\n    C10_LOG_API_USAGE_ONCE(\"ProcessGroupNCCL.WorkNCCL.handleException\");\n\n    auto logger = c10d::C10dLogger::getLogger();\n    if (logger) {\n      ::c10d::C10dLoggingData data;\n      data.strings[\"work_nccl_exception\"] =\n          getExceptionMsgFromExceptionPtr(exception_);\n      logger->log(data);\n    }\n\n    if (SHOULD_TEAR_DOWN(errorHandling)) {\n      auto tearDownMsg = c10::str(\n          \"To avoid data inconsistency, we are taking the entire process down.\");\n      LOG(ERROR) << logPrefix() << tearDownMsg;\n      std::rethrow_exception(exception_);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::synchronize() {\n  synchronizeStream();\n  if (c10d::allow_inflight_collective_as_graph_input()) {\n    c10d::unregister_work(\n        c10::intrusive_ptr<\n            ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL>::unsafe_reclaim_from_nonowning(this));\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::synchronizeStream() {\n  auto currentStream = at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream(device_.index());\n  // Block the current stream on the NCCL stream\n  ncclEndEvent_->block(currentStream);\n  // Unstage the stashed tensors so that CachingAllocator can recycle them\n  // THIS MUST HAPPEN AFTER THE BLOCKING CALL ABOVE\n  stashed_for_allocator_safety_->unstash();\n}\n\n// Same as calling synchronize() when blockingWait_ is false\nbool ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::wait(std::chrono::milliseconds timeout) {\n  RECORD_PARAM_COMMS(\n      std::make_tuple(static_cast<int64_t>(this->seq_), this->isP2P_), // seq\n      std::make_tuple(pgUID_, pgDesc_), // PG name tuple\n      rank_, // rank\n      \"wait\", // collective name\n      0, // inNelems\n      0, // outNelems\n      at::kByte, // dType\n      std::vector<int64_t>(), // inSplitSizes\n      std::vector<int64_t>(), // outSplitSizes\n      -1,\n      -1,\n      static_cast<int>(1)); // number of device?\n\n  // synchronize() will block the current stream on the NCCL stream\n  synchronize();\n\n  // In case of blockingWait or a timeout value is specified by the user, we\n  // block the CPU thread until the work is completed or timed out.\n  if (blockingWait_ || timeout != kNoTimeout) {\n    while (!isCompleted()) {\n      bool timedOut = checkTimeout(\n          timeout == kNoTimeout ? std::nullopt : std::make_optional(timeout));\n      // Explicitly abort ncclComms here before throwing this timed out\n      // exception to users.\n      // If throwing timed out excepiton without aborting nccl communicators\n      // here, it was observed that CUDA GPU will have 100% utilization and\n      // can not run new events successfully.\n      if (timedOut) {\n        std::string exceptionMsg = c10::str(\n            logPrefix(), \"Work \", (*this), \" timed out in blocking wait.\");\n        LOG(ERROR) << exceptionMsg;\n        break;\n      }\n      // Yield\n      std::this_thread::sleep_for(\n          std::chrono::milliseconds(kSynchronizeBusyWaitMillis));\n    }\n  } else if (isBarrierOp_ && !isCompleted()) {\n    // For barrier wait when timeout is unspecified, we block the CPU thread on\n    // current stream. This is to minimize the CPU barrier wait time in healthy\n    // path\n    auto currentStream = at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream(device_.index());\n    // CUDAStream wrapper will correctly use a DeviceGuard here\n    currentStream.synchronize();\n  }\n\n  // If exception is detected, throw it from the main CPU thread\n  if (exception()) {\n    // Abort NCCL communicators\n    abort();\n    // Throw exception (from main thread here)\n    handleException(TearDown);\n  }\n\n  // TODO(kwen2501): this should be moved to c10d tests, to qualify a NCCL\n  // upgrade. Once a NCCL version is qualified, this code should not be needed\n  // at runtime.\n#ifdef PGNCCL_ENABLE_HASH\n  if (enableCollectiveHashDebug_.load()) {\n    auto numel = getTensorsNumel(*outputs_);\n    auto hashValue = hashTensors(*outputs_);\n    PRINT_COLLECTIVE_HASH_SIGNATURE(\n        \"output\", opTypeToString(opType_), numel, hashValue);\n  }\n#endif // PGNCCL_ENABLE_HASH\n  // Always return true, because abort API is not implemented.\n  return true;\n}\n\nvoid ProcessGroupNCCL::WorkNCCL::abort() {\n  // dump before aborting for rcclexp\n#if defined(USE_ROCM) && defined(NCCL_COMM_DUMP)\n  auto dumpMap = ncclComm_->ncclCommDump();\n  printNcclCommProxyTrace(\"WorkNCCL::abort\", dumpMap);\n#endif // USE_ROCM && NCCL_COMM_DUMP\n\n  // Abort all communicators of this work\n  ncclComm_->abort();\n\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(ncclCommMemPoolMapMutex);\n    ncclCommMemPoolMap.erase(ncclComm_);\n  }\n}\n\nstatic std::atomic<size_t> process_group_id = 0;\n\nconstexpr const char* MULTI_DEVICE_ERROR_MSG =\n    \"Expecting one tensor only but got multiple. You are probably using multiple \"\n    \"devices under one thread. The support for such usage has been deprecated. \"\n    \"For details, please refer to \"\n    \"https://pytorch.org/docs/stable/distributed.html#multi-gpu-collective-functions. \"\n    \"ProcessGroupNCCL continues supporting multi-process and multi-thread modes.\";\n\nProcessGroupNCCL::ProcessGroupNCCL(\n    c10::intrusive_ptr<Store> store,\n    int rank,\n    int size,\n    c10::intrusive_ptr<Options> options)\n    : Backend(rank, size),\n      store_(std::move(store)),\n      options_(std::move(options)),\n      terminateProcessGroup_(false),\n      local_id_(process_group_id++),\n      intraNodeComm_(initIntraNodeComm()) {\n  TORCH_CHECK_WITH(\n      ValueError,\n      at::cuda::getNumGPUs() != 0,\n      \"ProcessGroupNCCL is only supported with GPUs, no GPUs found!\");\n\n  // getNcclVersion needs to get called before launching threads which can\n  // potentially call getenv. getNcclVersion internally calls setenv to set some\n  // environment variables from config file, which can race with getenv from\n  // other threads and cause segfaults.\n  const auto ncclVersion = getNcclVersion();\n  this->setGroupUid(options_->group_name);\n  this->localDeviceCount_ = static_cast<int>(at::cuda::getNumGPUs());\n  logPrefix_ = createLogPrefix();\n  blockingWait_ = getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_BLOCKING_WAIT, false);\n  asyncErrorHandling_ = static_cast<ErrorHandlingMode>(\n      getCvarInt(TORCH_NCCL_ASYNC_ERROR_HANDLING, 3 /*SkipCleanUp*/));\n  enableNanCheck_ = getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_NAN_CHECK, false);\n  cudaEventCacheEnabled_.store(getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_CUDA_EVENT_CACHE, true));\n  traceBufferSize_ = getCvarInt(TORCH_NCCL_TRACE_BUFFER_SIZE, 2000);\n  enableCollectiveHashDebug_ = (dist_debug_level_ >= DebugLevel::Detail);\n  // store_ usually is wrapped with PrefixStore and the prefix is different\n  // across different ProcessGroupNCCL(PG) instances. We need to get the\n  // underlying non-PrefixStore for sharing global information shared across\n  // different PGs.\n  PrefixStore* prefixStore = dynamic_cast<PrefixStore*>(store_.get());\n  globalStore_ =\n      prefixStore ? prefixStore->getUnderlyingNonPrefixStore() : store_;\n  auto desyncDebug = getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_DESYNC_DEBUG, false) ||\n      (dist_debug_level_ >= DebugLevel::Detail);\n#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING\n  enableTiming_.store(\n      getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_ENABLE_TIMING, false) || desyncDebug);\n#endif // ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING\n  if (getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_AVOID_RECORD_STREAMS, false)) {\n    TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\n        \"TORCH_NCCL_AVOID_RECORD_STREAMS is the default now, this environment variable is thus deprecated.\");\n  }\n  showSerializationWarning_ =\n      getCvarBool(TORCH_NCCL_SHOW_EAGER_INIT_P2P_SERIALIZATION_WARNING, true);\n\n  if (blockingWait_) {\n    LOG(INFO)\n        << logPrefix()\n        << \"TORCH_NCCL_BLOCKING_WAIT is enabled, NO watchdog thread is created.\";\n  } else {\n    if (desyncDebug && asyncErrorHandling_ == NoHandling) {\n      LOG(INFO)\n          << logPrefix()\n          << \"TORCH_NCCL_DESYNC_DEBUG and TORCH_NCCL_ASYNC_ERROR_HANDLING \"\n          << \"must both be enabled. \"\n          << \"Enabling TORCH_NCCL_ASYNC_ERROR_HANDLING.\";\n      asyncErrorHandling_ = SkipCleanUp;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // If deterministic mode is enabled, we need to disable the NVLS algorithm in\n  // NCCL.\n  // TODO: remove this once NVLS supports deterministic mode.\n  if (at::globalContext().deterministicAlgorithms()) {\n    // Check if user have already set NCCL_ALGO. This is a blocking function.\n// Arguments:\n//   longInterval: if true, wait with sleep of an interval; otherwise, wait\n//   with `sched_yield` which is faster (but acquires CPU more frequently).\nvoid NCCLComm::waitReady(bool longInterval) {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  if (aborted_)\n    return;\n  // If timeout is reached, throw an exception.\n  // (RohitRathore1) Note: We already hold the mutex_ lock here, so the direct\n  // call to ncclCommGetAsyncError is safe from concurrent access.\n  ncclResult_t result = ncclInProgress;\n  auto startTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n  auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();\n  while (result == ncclInProgress) {\n    auto currentTime = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n    auto timeElapsed = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::seconds>(\n                           currentTime - startTimepoint)\n                           .count();\n    if (timeElapsed > timeout) {\n      std::string err = \"NCCL timeout in: \" + std::string(__FILE__) + \":\" +\n          std::to_string(__LINE__);\n      TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);\n    }\n    if (longInterval) {\n      std::this_thread::sleep_for(\n          std::chrono::milliseconds(kCommInitBusyWaitMillis));\n    } else {\n      sched_yield();\n    }\n    ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &result);\n  }\n  if (result != ncclSuccess) {\n    std::string err = \"NCCL error in: \" + std::string(__FILE__) + \":\" +\n        std::to_string(__LINE__) + \", \" + ncclGetErrorWithVersion(result) +\n        \"\\n\" + getNcclErrorDetailStr(result, std::nullopt);\n    TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);\n  }\n}",

this->uniqueHash_ = std::move(hash);\n}\n\nstd::string NCCLComm::getUniqueHash() {\n  return uniqueHash_;\n}\n\nstd::shared_ptr<NCCLComm> NCCLComm::create(\n    int numRanks,\n    int rank,\n    ncclUniqueId commId,\n    at::DeviceIndex deviceIndex) {\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex);\n  auto comm = std::make_shared<NCCLComm>();\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n      ncclCommInitRank(&(comm->ncclComm_), numRanks, commId, rank),\n      std::nullopt);\n  comm->setUniqueHash(commId);\n  comm->rank_ = rank;\n  comm->deviceIndex_ = deviceIndex;\n  comm->initialized_ = true;\n  // Old style comm is always blocking.\n  comm->nonBlocking_ = false;\n  return comm;\n}\n\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_CONFIG\nstd::shared_ptr<NCCLComm> NCCLComm::create(\n    int numRanks,\n    int rank,\n    ncclUniqueId commId,\n    at::DeviceIndex deviceIndex,\n    ncclConfig_t& config) {\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex);\n  auto comm = std::make_shared<NCCLComm>();\n  comm->nonBlocking_ = config.blocking == 0;\n  LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << rank << \": creating NCCL communicator with mode: \"\n            << (comm->nonBlocking_ ? \"nonblocking\" : \"blocking\");\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_NONBLOCKING(\n      ncclCommInitRankConfig(\n          &(comm->ncclComm_), numRanks, commId, rank, &config),\n      std::nullopt);\n  comm->setUniqueHash(commId);\n  comm->rank_ = rank;\n  comm->deviceIndex_ = deviceIndex;\n  // Under blocking mode, comm is initialized immediately after NCCL init\n  // returns; Under nonblocking mode, we check whether comm is initialized the\n  // *next* time ncclComm_ is accessed.\n  comm->initialized_ = !comm->nonBlocking_;\n  return comm;\n}\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_INIT_RANK_SCALABLE\nstd::shared_ptr<NCCLComm> NCCLComm::create_scalable(\n    int numRanks,\n    int rank,\n    std::vector<ncclUniqueId>& commIds,\n    at::DeviceIndex deviceIndex,\n    ncclConfig_t& config) {\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex);\n  auto comm = std::make_shared<NCCLComm>();\n  comm->nonBlocking_ = config.blocking == 0;\n  LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << rank << \": creating NCCL communicator with mode: \"\n            << (comm->nonBlocking_ ?  rank,\n          commIds.size(),\n          commIds.data(),\n          &config),\n      std::nullopt);\n  // Only the first ncclUniqueId will be used to create the\n  // communicator hash id, which auto commFailureMsg = commFailureReason_ != std::nullopt\n        ? c10::str(\" Original reason for failure was: \", *commFailureReason_)\n        : \"\";\n    TORCH_CHECK_WITH(\n        DistBackendError,\n        false,\n        c10::str(\n            \"NCCL communicator was aborted on rank \",\n            rank_,\n            \". \",\n            commFailureMsg));\n  }\n  // In non-blocking mode, ensure comm is ready.\n  if (nonBlocking_) {\n    // Wait with long interval if communicator is being initialized.\n    bool longInterval = !initialized_;\n    waitReady(longInterval);\n    // ncclComm_ should be initialized by now\n  }\n  if (!initialized_) {\n    // TODO: see if we can consolidate other `initialized_` flipping here.\n    // Maintaining it elsewhere is some work.\n    initialized_ = true;\n    LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << rank_ << \": NCCL communicator \" << repr()\n              << \" is initialized.\";\n  }\n  return ncclComm_;\n}\n\nat::DeviceIndex NCCLComm::getDeviceIndex() {\n  return deviceIndex_;\n}\n\n// Wait for the communicator to be ready. This is a blocking function.\n// Arguments:\n//   longInterval: if true, wait with sleep of an interval; otherwise, wait\n//   with `sched_yield` which is faster (but acquires CPU more frequently).\nvoid NCCLComm::waitReady(bool longInterval) {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  if (aborted_)\n    return;\n  // If timeout is reached, throw an exception.\n  // (RohitRathore1) Note: We already hold the mutex_ lock here, so the direct\n  // call to ncclCommGetAsyncError is safe from concurrent access.\n  ncclResult_t result = ncclInProgress;\n  auto startTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n  auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();\n  while (result == ncclInProgress) {\n    auto currentTime = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n    auto timeElapsed = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::seconds>(\n                           currentTime - startTimepoint)\n                           .count();\n    if (timeElapsed > timeout) {\n      std::string err = \"NCCL timeout in: \" + std::string(__FILE__) + \":\" +\n          std::to_string(__LINE__);\n      TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);\n    }\n    if (longInterval) {\n      std::this_thread::sleep_for(\n          std::chrono::milliseconds(kCommInitBusyWaitMillis));\n    } else {\n      sched_yield();\n    }\n    ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &result);\n  }\n  if (result != ncclSuccess) {\n    std::string err = \"NCCL error in: \" + std::string(__FILE__) + \":\" +\n        std::to_string(__LINE__) + \", \" + ncclGetErrorWithVersion(result) +\n        \"\\n\" + getNcclErrorDetailStr(result, std::nullopt);\n    TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);\n  }\n}\n\nstd::optional<std::string> NCCLComm::getNcclCommFailureReason() const {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  return commFailureReason_;\n}\n\n#if defined(NCCL_HAS_COMM_SPLIT)\nstd::shared_ptr<NCCLComm> NCCLComm::split(\n    NCCLComm* source,\n    int color_id,\n    int rank,\n    ncclConfig_t& config) {\n  TORCH_CHECK(\n      color_id >= NCCL_SPLIT_NOCOLOR,\n      \"Color must be a non-negative value or NCCL_SPLIT_NOCOLOR (-1)\"\n      \", but got \",\n      color_id);\n  LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << source->rank_ << \": split from parent comm \"\n            << source->repr() << \" with color_id \" << color_id << \" and rank \"\n            << rank;\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(source->deviceIndex_);\n  auto comm = std::make_shared<NCCLComm>();\n  // This call will block until the source communicator is initialized\n  auto sourceComm = source->getNcclComm();\n#ifndef NCCL_HAS_COMM_NONBLOCKING\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n      ncclCommSplit(sourceComm, color_id, rank, &(comm->ncclComm_), &config),\n      std::nullopt);\n#else\n  // After calling ncclCommSplit in non-blocking mode, we should wait for the\n  // source communicator to be out of ncclInProgress state.\n  // Reason 1:\n  //   it's unsafe to call new operations on the parent comm while it's in\n  //   ncclInProgress state.\n  // Reason 2:\n  //   as of NCCL 2.23, the ptr value of child comm will not be filled until the\n  //   state of parent comm is ncclSuccess. This may change in the future. See:\n  //   https://github.com/NVIDIA/nccl/issues/1472\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_SLEEP(\n      ncclCommSplit(sourceComm, color_id, rank, &(comm->ncclComm_), &config),\n      sourceComm, // wait on parent comm\n      std::nullopt);\n  if (color_id >= 0) {\n    // Waiting for parent comm above still does not seem to guarantee the child\n    // comm ptr is valid. Therefore we add a manual wait here for safety.\n    // TODO: remove this wait after NCCL fix the semantics.\n    auto startTime = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n    auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();\n    while (!comm->ncclComm_) {\n      C10D_CHECK_TIMEOUT(startTime, timeout);\n      C10D_SCHED_SLEEP();\n    }\n  }\n  // comm->ncclComm_ should have valid ptr by now, but not necessarily\n  // initialized. Rely on getNcclComm() to wait for its initialization.\n#endif\n  ++source->ncclCommSplitCounter_;\n  comm->rank_ = rank;\n  // Child comm should be on the same device as parent comm\n  comm->deviceIndex_ = source->deviceIndex_;\n  comm->nonBlocking_ = config.blocking == 0;\n  comm->setUniqueHash(\n      source->getUniqueHash() + \":\" +\n      std::to_string(source->ncclCommSplitCounter_));\n  LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << source->rank_ << \": created child comm \"\n            << comm->repr() << \" with color_id \" << color_id;\n  return comm;\n}\n#endif\n\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_SHRINK\nstd::shared_ptr<NCCLComm> NCCLComm::shrink(\n    NCCLComm* source,\n    std::vector<int>& ranks_to_exclude,\n    ncclConfig_t* config,\n    int shrinkFlags) {\n  // Preconditions are validated in ProcessGroupNCCL::shrink\n\n  LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << source->rank_ << \": shrinking comm \" << source->repr()\n            << \" excluding \" << ranks_to_exclude.size() << \" ranks\";\n\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(source->deviceIndex_);\n  auto comm = std::make_shared<NCCLComm>();\n\n  // This call will block until the source communicator is initialized\n  auto sourceComm = source->getNcclComm();\n\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_NONBLOCKING(\n      ncclCommShrink(\n          sourceComm,\n          ranks_to_exclude.data(),\n          ranks_to_exclude.size(),\n          reinterpret_cast<ncclComm_t*>(&(comm->ncclComm_)),\n          config,\n          shrinkFlags),\n      source->getNcclCommFailureReason());\n\n  // Wait for the child communicator to be ready\n  source->waitReady(true);\n  comm->initialized_ = true;\n\n  // NCCL automatically assigns rank during shrink - Skip finalize.\";\n    return;\n  }\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex_);\n  auto comm = getNcclComm();\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_NONBLOCKING(ncclCommFinalize(comm), std::nullopt);\n}\n\nvoid NCCLComm::destroy() {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  if (aborted_) {\n    LOG(INFO) << \"Rank \" << rank_\n              << \": NCCL communicator already Invalidated. Skip destroy.\";\n    return;\n  }\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex_);\n  auto comm = getNcclComm();\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(ncclCommDestroy(comm), std::nullopt);\n  // Poison future getNcclComm\n  aborted_ = true;\n}\n\nvoid NCCLComm::abort(std::optional<std::string> commFailureReason) {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex_);\n#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING\n  if (aborted_ && !initialized_) {\n    // Should not abort twice.\n    return;\n  }\n\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER\n  // Deregister all registered segments before aborting.\n  for (auto& it : registeredSegmentHandles_) {\n    void* handle = it.second;\n    C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n        ::ncclCommDeregister(ncclComm_, handle),\n        c10::str(\n            \"Failed to deregister segment handle \",\n            handle,\n            \" on ncclComm_ \",\n            ncclComm_));\n  }\n  registeredSegmentHandles_.clear();\n#endif\n\n  // Set true failure reason if provided by ProcessGroupNCCL (e.g. work\n  // timeout)\n  commFailureReason_ = commFailureReason;\n  LOG(INFO) << \"Aborting ncclComm_ \" << ncclComm_ << \" with reason: \"\n            << (commFailureReason ? *commFailureReason\n                                  : \"No abort reason provided.\");\n#ifndef NCCL_HAS_COMM_NONBLOCKING\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(::ncclCommAbort(ncclComm_), commFailureReason_);\n#else\n  // Note: We already hold the mutex_ lock here, so the direct call to\n  // ncclCommGetAsyncError is safe from concurrent access.\n  ncclResult_t result = ::ncclCommAbort(ncclComm_);\n  auto startTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n  auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();\n  while (result == ncclInProgress) {\n    auto currentTime = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n    auto timeElapsed = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::seconds>(\n                           currentTime - startTimepoint)\n                           .count();\n    if (timeElapsed > timeout) {\n      std::string err = \"NCCL timeout in: \" + std::string(__FILE__) + \":\" +\n          std::to_string(__LINE__);\n      TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);\n    }\n    sched_yield();\n    ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &result);\n  }\n  if (result != ncclSuccess) {\n    std::string err = \"NCCL error in: \" + std::string(__FILE__) + \":\" +\n        std::to_string(__LINE__) + \", \" + ncclGetErrorWithVersion(result) +\n        \"\\n\" + getNcclErrorDetailStr(result, commFailureReason_);\n    TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);\n  }\n#endif\n  aborted_ = true;\n  ncclComm_ = nullptr;\n\n  // Set an appropriate error so that we avoid using the communicator.\n  if (ncclAsyncErr_ == ncclSuccess) {\n    ncclAsyncErr_ = ncclSystemError;\n  }\n#else\n  // This is a NOOP, if error checks are disabled.\n  return;\n#endif\n}\n\nbool NCCLComm::isInitialized() const {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  return initialized_;\n}\n\nbool NCCLComm::isAborted() const {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n  return aborted_;\n}\n\nuint64_t NCCLComm::getCommSplitCounter() const {\n  return ncclCommSplitCounter_;\n}\n\nncclResult_t NCCLComm::checkForNcclError() {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING\n  if (ncclAsyncErr_ != ncclSuccess) {\n    return ncclAsyncErr_;\n  }\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n      ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &ncclAsyncErr_), commFailureReason_);\n  return ncclAsyncErr_;\n#else\n  // Always return success, if error checks are disabled.\n  return ncclSuccess;\n#endif\n}\n\nncclResult_t NCCLComm::registerSegment(\n    void* ptr,\n    size_t size,\n    bool errorOnRereg, /*=true*/\n    bool window /*=false*/) {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER\n  // We register only segments from cache allocator\n  // which are guaranteed to be with disjoint addr ranges. Thus, a ptr always\n  // maps to a unique handle and should not be registered before the current\n  // ptr is deregistered and freed.\n  if (registeredSegmentHandles_.count(ptr) > 0) {\n ncclSuccess;\n  }\n\n  void* handle = nullptr;\n  // Use getNcclComm to make sure comm is ready before calling nccl APIs\n  auto comm = getNcclComm();\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_WINDOW_REGISTER\n  if (window) {\n    C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n        ncclCommWindowRegister(\n            comm, ptr, size, (ncclWindow_t*)&handle, NCCL_WIN_COLL_SYMMETRIC),\n        c10::str(\n            \"Failed to window ncclComm_ \",\n            comm));\n  }\n#else\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n      ncclCommRegister(comm, ptr, size, &handle),\n      c10::str(\n          \"Failed to register segment with ptr \",\n          ptr,\n          \", size \",\n          size,\n          \" on ncclComm_ \",\n          comm));\n#endif\n  registeredSegmentHandles_[ptr] = handle;\n  return ncclSuccess;\n#else\n  return ncclInvalidUsage;\n#endif\n}\n\nncclResult_t NCCLComm::deregisterSegment(void* ptr, bool window /*false*/) {\n  LockType lock(mutex_);\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER\n  TORCH_CHECK(\n      registeredSegmentHandles_.count(ptr) == 1,\n      \"Segment with ptr \",\n      ptr,\n      \" is not registered on ncclComm_ \",\n      ncclComm_);\n\n  void* handle = registeredSegmentHandles_[ptr];\n  // Use getNcclComm to make sure comm is ready before calling nccl APIs\n  auto comm = getNcclComm();\n#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_WINDOW_REGISTER\n  if (window) {\n    C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n        ncclCommWindowDeregister(comm, (ncclWindow_t)handle),\n        c10::str(\n            \"Failed to window deregister segment handle \",\n            handle,\n            \", with ptr \",\n            ptr,\n            \" on ncclComm_ \",\n            comm));\n  } else {\n    C10D_NCCL_CHECK(\n        ncclCommDeregister(comm, handle),\n        c10::str(\n \",\n          comm));\n#endif\n  registeredSegmentHandles_.erase(ptr);\n  return ncclSuccess;\n#else\n  return ncclInvalidUsage;\n#endif\n}\n\nstd::string NCCLComm::repr() const {\n  return c10::str((void*)ncclComm_);\n}\n\n#if (defined(IS_NCCLX) || defined(USE_ROCM)) && defined(NCCL_COMM_DUMP)\nstd::unordered_map<std::string, std::string> NCCLComm::ncclCommDump() {\n  std::unordered_map<std::string, std::string> dump;\n  if (isAborted()) {\n    LOG(INFO) << \"Communicator was aborted before trying to dump its state.\";\n    return dump;\n  }\n  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(::ncclCommDump(ncclComm_, dump), std::nullopt);\n  return dump;\n}\n#endif\n\nstd::string getNcclVersion() {\n  static std::string versionString = []() {\n    auto [ncclMajor, ncclMinor, ncclPatch] = getNcclVersionTuple();\n    std::string versionString;\n    if (ncclMajor == 0 && ncclMinor == 0 && ncclPatch == 0) {\n      versionString = \"Unknown NCCL version\";\n    } else {\n      versionString = std::to_string(ncclMajor) + \".\" +\n          std::to_string(ncclMinor) + \".\" + std::to_string(ncclPatch);\n#ifdef NCCL_SUFFIX\n      const auto ncclSuffix = std::string(NCCL_SUFFIX);\n      if (!ncclSuffix.empty()) {\n        versionString += \".\" + ncclSuffix;\n      }\n#endif\n    }\n    return versionString;\n  }();\n\n  return versionString;\n}\n\nstd::tuple<int, int, int> getNcclVersionTuple() {\n  static std::tuple<int, int, int> versionTuple = []() {\n    int version = getNcclVersionNumber();\n    // can't compute the version if call did not return successfully or version\n    // code < 100 (corresponding to 0.1.0)\n    if (version < 100) {\n      return std::make_tuple(0, 0, 0);\n    }\n    // NCCL changed version coding starting 2.9\n    const int majorBase = version < 2900 ? 1000 : 10000;\n    const int minorBase = 100;\n    auto ncclMajor = version / majorBase;\n    auto ncclMinor = (version % majorBase) / minorBase;\n    auto ncclPatch = version % minorBase;\n    return std::make_tuple(ncclMajor, ncclMinor, ncclPatch);\n  }();\n  return versionTuple;\n}\n\nint getNcclVersionNumber() {\n  static int version = []() {\n    int version = 0;\n    ncclResult_t status = ncclGetVersion(&version);\n    if (status != ncclSuccess) {\n      return 0; // Error.\n    }\n    return version;\n  }();\n  return version;\n}\n\nsize_t hashTensors(const std::vector<at::Tensor>& tensors) {\n  size_t hash = 0;\n  for (auto& tensor : tensors) {\n    if (tensor.numel() > 0 && tensor.storage()) {\n      size_t data_size = tensor.storage().nbytes();\n      if (data_size > 0 && tensor.storage().data_ptr()) {\n        auto src = static_cast<const char*>(tensor.storage().data_ptr().get());\n        std::vector<char> dst(data_size);\n        // This is needed so that we trigger a device synchronization so we can\n        // get the collective finished if launched on GPU and hash its output.\n        AT_CUDA_CHECK(\n            cudaMemcpy(dst.data(), src, data_size, cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < data_size; ++i) {\n          // Update the hash for each byte in the tensor\n          hash = c10::hash_combine(hash, c10::get_hash(dst[i], data_size));\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  return hash;\n}\n\n// NCCL uses Non-negative int to represent in-group according to API\n// requirement. We take a list of ranks and generate a hash value based on the\n// list and ensure its range of 32-bit int.\nint genNcclSplitColor(const std::vector<int>& ranks) {\n  // Combine the hash values using a simple reducer (std::hash + fold)\n  std::size_t combined_hash = std::accumulate(\n      ranks.begin(),\n      ranks.end(),\n      std::size_t(0),\n      [](std::size_t acc, int rank) {\n        return acc ^\n            (std::hash<int>{}(rank) + 0x9e3779b9 + (acc << 6) + (acc >> 2));\n      });\n\n  // max positive value of int32_t\n  constexpr int32_t max_c_int = std::numeric_limits<int32_t>::max();\n  int color = static_cast<int>(\n      std::abs(static_cast<int64_t>(combined_hash)) % max_c_int);\n  return color;\n}\n\n// Default value: 30 minutes\nint nccl_nonblocking_timeout() {\n  static int timeout = -2; // -2 means not initialized\n  if (timeout == -2) {\n    const auto val = c10::utils::get_env(\"TORCH_NCCL_NONBLOCKING_TIMEOUT\");\n    if (val.has_value() && !val.value().empty()) {\n      timeout = stoi(val.value());\n    } else {\n      // Default value consistent with kBackendDefaultTimeout\n      timeout = 30 * 60;\n    }\n  }\n  return timeout;\n}\n\nstd::string ncclGetErrorWithVersion(ncclResult_t error) {\n  return std::string(ncclGetErrorString(error)) + \", NCCL version \" +\n      getNcclVersion();\n}\n\n// Provides additional detail into NCCL error codes based on when these are\n// thrown in the NCCL codebase.\nstd::string getNcclErrorDetailStr(\n    ncclResult_t error,\n    std::optional<std::string> processGroupFailureReason /* = std::nullopt */\n) {\n  // Prioritize failure reason provided by PG NCCL first, as it can abort\n  // communicators when it encounters collective timeouts, etc.\n  if (processGroupFailureReason != std::nullopt) {\n    return *processGroupFailureReason;\n  }\n  std::string interpret;\n  std::string err;\n#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_GET_LAST_ERROR\n  auto ret = ncclGetLastError(nullptr);\n  if (ret) {\n    err = \"\\nLast error:\\n\" + std::string(ret);\n  } else {\n    err = \"\\nLast error: Unknown NCCL Error\\n\";\n  }\n#endif\n  switch (error) {\n    case ncclUnhandledCudaError:\n      interpret = \"ncclUnhandledCudaError: Call to CUDA function failed.\";\n      break;\n    case ncclSystemError:\n      interpret =\n          \"ncclSystemError: System call (e.g. socket, malloc) or external library call failed or device error. \";\n#ifndef NCCL_REMOTE_ERROR\n      // Before ncclRemoteError was created, unexpected remote disconnect was\n      // categorized as ncclSystemError\n      interpret += \"It can be also caused by unexpected exit of a remote peer.\";\n#endif\n      break;\n    case ncclInternalError:\n      interpret = // Macro to throw on a non-successful NCCL return value, non-blocking.
#define C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE(cmd, comm, failureReason, yield_fn)      \
  do {                                                                        \
    ncclResult_t result = cmd;                                                \
    auto startTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();                   \
    auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();                                \
    while (result == ncclInProgress) {                                        \
      C10D_CHECK_TIMEOUT(startTimepoint, timeout);                            \
      yield_fn;                                                               \
      ncclCommGetAsyncError(comm, &result);                                   \
    }                                                                         \
    if (result != ncclSuccess) {                                              \
      std::string err = "NCCL error in: " + std::string(__FILE__) + ":" +     \
          std::to_string(__LINE__) + ", " + ncclGetErrorWithVersion(result) + \
          "\n" + getNcclErrorDetailStr(result, failureReason);                \
      TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);                         \
    }                                                                         \
  } while (0)
After
// Macro to throw on a non-successful NCCL return value, non-blocking.
// Thread-safe: uses NCCLComm wrapper's getAsyncError() which acquires mutex
// before calling ncclCommGetAsyncError to prevent race conditions between
// watchdog and main threads.
#define C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE(                                         \
    cmd, commWrapper, failureReason, yield_fn)                                \
  do {                                                                        \
    ncclResult_t result = cmd;                                                \
    auto startTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();                   \
    auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();                                \
    while (result == ncclInProgress) {                                        \
      C10D_CHECK_TIMEOUT(startTimepoint, timeout);                            \
      yield_fn;                                                               \
      commWrapper->getAsyncError(&result);                                    \
    }                                                                         \
    if (result != ncclSuccess) {                                              \
      std::string err = "NCCL error in: " + std::string(__FILE__) + ":" +     \
          std::to_string(__LINE__) + ", " + ncclGetErrorWithVersion(result) + \
          "\n" + getNcclErrorDetailStr(result, failureReason);                \
      TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);                         \
    }                                                                         \
  } while (0)
2. EDIT /workspace/torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.hpp
Before
// Macro to throw exception on a non-successful NCCL return value or timeout.
// This macro uses sched_yield() to yield the CPU.
// Thus suitable for NCCL calls that would quickly turn ncclSuccess, e.g.
// collectives.
#define C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT(cmd, comm, failureReason) \
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE(cmd, comm, failureReason, sched_yield())

// Macro to throw exception on a non-successful NCCL return value or timeout.
// This macro uses sleep to yield the CPU.
// Thus suitable for NCCL calls that would take longer to turn ncclSuccess, e.g.
// ncclCommInitRankConfig, ncclCommFinalize, etc.
#define C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_SLEEP(cmd, comm, failureReason) \
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE(cmd, comm, failureReason, C10D_SCHED_SLEEP())
After
// Macro to throw exception on a non-successful NCCL return value or timeout.

// Thus suitable for NCCL calls that would quickly turn ncclSuccess, e.g.

#define C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT(cmd, commWrapper, failureReason) \
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE(cmd, commWrapper, failureReason, sched_yield())

5. EDIT /workspace/torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.cpp
Before
// Wait for the communicator to be ready. This is a blocking function.
// Arguments:
//   longInterval: if true, wait with sleep of an interval; otherwise, wait
//   with `sched_yield` which is faster (but acquires CPU more frequently).
void NCCLComm::waitReady(bool longInterval) {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
  if (aborted_)
    return;
  // If timeout is reached, throw an exception.
  if (longInterval) {
    C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_SLEEP(ncclInProgress, ncclComm_, std::nullopt);
  } else {
    C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT(ncclInProgress, ncclComm_, std::nullopt);
  }
}
After
// Wait for the communicator to be ready. This is a blocking function.
// Arguments:
//   longInterval: if true, wait with sleep of an interval; otherwise, wait
//   with `sched_yield` which is faster (but acquires CPU more frequently).
void NCCLComm::waitReady(bool longInterval) {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
  if (aborted_)
    return;
  // If timeout is reached, throw an exception.
  // (RohitRathore1) Note: We already hold the mutex_ lock here, so the direct
  // call to ncclCommGetAsyncError is safe from concurrent access.
  ncclResult_t result = ncclInProgress;
  auto startTimepoint = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
  auto timeout = nccl_nonblocking_timeout();
  while (result == ncclInProgress) {
    auto currentTime = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();
    auto timeElapsed = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::seconds>(
                           currentTime - startTimepoint)
                           .count();
    if (timeElapsed > timeout) {
      std::string err = "NCCL timeout in: " + std::string(__FILE__) + ":" +
          std::to_string(__LINE__);
      TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);
    }
    if (longInterval) {
      std::this_thread::sleep_for(
          std::chrono::milliseconds(kCommInitBusyWaitMillis));
    } else {
      sched_yield();
    }
    ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &result);
  }
  if (result != ncclSuccess) {
    std::string err = "NCCL error in: " + std::string(__FILE__) + ":" +
        std::to_string(__LINE__) + ", " + ncclGetErrorWithVersion(result) +
        "\n" + getNcclErrorDetailStr(result, std::nullopt);
    TORCH_CHECK_WITH(DistBackendError, false, err);
  }
}
6. EDIT /workspace/torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.cpp
Before
void NCCLComm::abort(std::optional<std::string> commFailureReason) {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex_);
#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING
  if (aborted_ && !initialized_) {
    // Should not abort twice.
    return;
  }

#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER
  // Deregister all registered segments before aborting.
  for (auto& it : registeredSegmentHandles_) {
    void* handle = it.second;
    C10D_NCCL_CHECK(
        ::ncclCommDeregister(ncclComm_, handle),
        c10::str(
            "Failed to deregister segment handle ",
            handle,
            " on ncclComm_ ",
            ncclComm_));
  }
  registeredSegmentHandles_.clear();
#endif

  // Set true failure reason if provided by ProcessGroupNCCL (e.g. work
  // timeout)
  commFailureReason_ = commFailureReason;
  LOG(INFO) << "Aborting ncclComm_ " << ncclComm_ << " with reason: "
            << (commFailureReason ? *commFailureReason
                                  : "No abort reason provided.");
#ifndef NCCL_HAS_COMM_NONBLOCKING
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(::ncclCommAbort(ncclComm_), commFailureReason_);
#else
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT(
      ::ncclCommAbort(ncclComm_), ncclComm_, commFailureReason_);
#endif
  aborted_ = true;
  ncclComm_ = nullptr;

  // Set an appropriate error so that we avoid using the communicator.
  if (ncclAsyncErr_ == ncclSuccess) {
    ncclAsyncErr_ = ncclSystemError;
  }
#else
  // This is a NOOP, if error checks are disabled.
  return;
#endif
}
After
void NCCLComm::abort(std::optional<std::string> commFailureReason) {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
  at::cuda::OptionalCUDAGuard gpuGuard(deviceIndex_);
#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING
  if (aborted_ && !initialized_) {
    // Should not abort twice.
    return;
  }

#ifdef NCCL_HAS_COMM_REGISTER
  // Deregister all registered segments before aborting.
  for (auto& it : registeredSegmentHandles_) {
    void* handle = it.second;
    C10D_NCCL_CHECK(
        ::ncclCommDeregister(ncclComm_, handle),
        c10::str(
            "Failed to deregister segment handle ",
            handle,
            " on ncclComm_ ",
            ncclComm_));
  }
  registeredSegmentHandles_.clear();
#endif

  // Set true failure reason if provided by ProcessGroupNCCL (e.g. work
  // timeout)
  commFailureReason_ = commFailureReason;
  LOG(INFO) << "Aborting ncclComm_ " << ncclComm_ << " with reason: "
            << (commFailureReason ? *commFailureReason
                                  : "No abort reason provided.");
#ifndef NCCL_HAS_COMM_NONBLOCKING
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(::ncclCommAbort(ncclComm_), commFailureReason_);
#else
  // Note: We already hold the mutex_ lock here, so the direct call to
  // ncclCommGetAsyncError is safe from concurrent access.

ncclResult_t NCCLComm::checkForNcclError() {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING
  if (ncclAsyncErr_ != ncclSuccess) {
    return ncclAsyncErr_;
  }
  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(
      ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &ncclAsyncErr_), commFailureReason_);
  return ncclAsyncErr_;
#else
  // Always return success, if error checks are disabled.
  return ncclSuccess;
#endif
}

ncclResult_t NCCLComm::checkForNcclError() {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
#ifdef ENABLE_NCCL_ERROR_CHECKING

    return ncclAsyncErr_;

  C10D_NCCL_CHECK(
      ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, &ncclAsyncErr_), commFailureReason_);

ncclResult_t NCCLComm::getAsyncError(ncclResult_t* asyncError) {
  LockType lock(mutex_);
  return ncclCommGetAsyncError(ncclComm_, asyncError);

2. $ git diff torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.hpp torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.cpp
3. $ make test 2>&1

5. $ git add torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.cpp torch/csrc/distributed/c10d/NCCLUtils.hpp
6. $ git commit -m "$(cat <<'EOF'
[c10d] Add thread safety when calling ncclCommGetAsyncError

Fixes #169484

This PR adds thread safety when calling ncclCommGetAsyncError to prevent
race conditions between the main thread and watchdog thread.

Changes:
- Added NCCLComm::getAsyncError() method that acquires mutex before
  calling ncclCommGetAsyncError
- Updated C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_BASE macro to use the thread-safe
  getAsyncError() wrapper instead of calling ncclCommGetAsyncError directly
- Updated C10D_NCCL_CHECK_TIMEOUT_GROUPEND macro similarly
- Rewrote NCCLComm::waitReady() to inline the loop (already holds mutex)
- Rewrote NCCLComm::abort() similarly (already holds mutex)
- Fixed NCCLComm::split() to pass NCCLComm* instead of ncclComm_t

The NCCL library does not provide thread-safety guarantees for
ncclCommGetAsyncError, so this change ensures concurrent access from
multiple threads (main thread and watchdog) is properly synchronized.

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.5 <noreply@anthropic.com>
EOF
)"
